***редактор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́ктор</a> (2203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">rédacteur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">editor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">redaktor</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">redáktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́кторы</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>редактора́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́кторов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>редакторо́в</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">реда́кторша</b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* uncommon</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">redáktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́кторы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редактор.html>реда́кторов</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> editor (person who edits)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> editor, processor; editing program</li></ol>

***редеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:редеть.html>реде́ть</a> (17270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rédkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-etʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редеть.html>реде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">redétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поредеть.html>пореде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thin, to thin out, to get thin</li>
<li>to be depleted, to thin out</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rědъkъ</i>. ***редко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>редко</a> (1732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rédkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rédko</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ре́дко" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ре́же</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rarely, seldom</li>
<li>sparsely</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***резать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a> (3175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рѣзати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rězati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rězati</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">рѣзати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rězati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">різати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rizaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">reža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">резати</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">rezati</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">řezat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">rezať</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rzezać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">rězać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">rězaś</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ῥήγνυμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rhḗgnumi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rézatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порезать.html>поре́зать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрезать.html>разре́зать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>заре́зать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срезать.html>сре́зать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut up, to cut open, to slice, to carve
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрезать.html>разре́зать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razrézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to slaughter, to knife, to kill
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>заре́зать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(on wood or metal)</i> to carve, to cut, to engrave</li>
<li>to cut off, to slice, to chop
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срезать.html>сре́зать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">srézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(on a test)</i> to give a failing grade
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срезать.html>сре́зать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">srézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(cause pain)</i> to hurt, to cut into</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to operate, to cut open</li>
<li>to irritate, to offend <i>(eyes)</i>, to grate on <i>(ears)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass close, to shave</li>
<li>to speak bluntly</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:срезать.html>сре́зать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:зарезать.html>заре́зать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:порезать.html>поре́зать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:разрезать.html>разре́зать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:перерезать.html>перере́зать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>вы́резать</a>, резнуть, <a href = vnd.unilang:резануть.html>резану́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объект</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:инструмент.html>инструмент</a> (твор. п.).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рез-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резаться.html>ре́заться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rézatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut, to be cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:резаться.html>ре́жется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">travá <b>réžetsja</b> lexkó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">grass <b>cuts</b> easily</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut through <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of teeth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:резаться.html>ре́жутся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u rebjónka <b>réžutsja</b> zúby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the child is teething</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">the child's teeth <b>are cutting through</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прорезаться.html>проре́заться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prorézatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fight with knives</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (a game) with passion <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — порезаться, <a href = vnd.unilang:прорезаться.html>проре́заться</a>, зарезаться, срезаться, разре́заться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рез-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***резвиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:резвиться.html>резви́ться</a> (16229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резвый.html>ре́звый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резвиться.html>резви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rezvítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to gambol, to frisk, to romp</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Accent pattern <i>c</i> (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резвиться.html>ре́звишься</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:резвиться.html>ре́звится</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:резвиться.html>ре́звятся</a></span>, etc.) was found in the older language<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1800</b>,  Gavrila Derzhavin,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>У́тро</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>Там</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:выплыть.html>вы́плыв</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пучина.html>пучи́ны</a>, // <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ют</a>, <b><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:резвиться.html>ре́звятся</a></strong></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дельфин.html>дельфи́ны</a>, // <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>рыб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стадо.html>стада́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверкать.html>сверка́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чешуя.html>чешуёй</a>, // <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>бле́щут</a> чуды <a href = vnd.unilang:чрево.html>чре́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белизна.html>белизно́й</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tam, výplyv iz pučíny, // Igrájut, <b>rézvjatsja</b> delʹfíny, // I ryb stadá sverkájut češujój, // I bléščut čudy čréva beliznój.</i></dd><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>

***резервация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:резервация.html>резерва́ция</a> (26703)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">reservātiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reservation, saving</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably by way of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">reservation</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резервация.html>резерва́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rezervácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резервация.html>резерва́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резервация.html>резерва́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резервация.html>резерва́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reservation <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in various senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>indigenous reservation</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:резец.html>резе́ц</a> (18657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рез(ать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rez(atʹ)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резец.html>резе́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rezéc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резец.html>резца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резец.html>резцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резец.html>резцо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cutter, cutting tool, chisel, draw knife</li>
<li>incisor <i>(tooth)</i></li>
<li>drill bit, tool bit</li>
<li>plow colter</li></ol>
